# File: region.txt

# This file holds templates for wilderness regions.

# The complete Middle-Earth map is currently 588 miles high by 882 miles wide. 
# y and x coordinates are for the top left of the region as shown in the D:
# lines (so in particular, that does include spaces).
# Each grid represents 1 square mile.
# Each square mile contains 10x10 portions of wilderness of 22x22 game grids.
# 3 of these 22x22 portions side by side makes up a world_chunk.

# N:region index:region name
# I:difficulty:height:width:y:x
# A:8 adjoining regions
# D:Map of the region using the following legend:
# + Forest
# - Lake
# ~ Ocean
# . Plain
# , Moor/Waste
# ^ Mountain
# _ Swamp
# | Dark Forest
# X Impassable Mountain
# W Impassable Water (Ocean)
# / Desert
# * Snow
# = Town
# & Landmark
